-->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">John in kala‑oh mul tawh a kigan puan silhin savun kawnggak tawh a kawng gak a, kauphe le gamlak khuaizu an in a nei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">Tua hun sungin hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"7\"><sup data-verseid=\"7\">&nbsp;<!-- -->7<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"7\">Pharisee pawlte le Sadducee pawlte tampi tui kiphum dinga hong pai John in a muh ciangin amaute kiangah, “A gupha gul suante aw, a hong tung ding Pasian hehna panin a kihemkhia dingin kua in hong hilhkhol ahi hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"8\"><sup data-verseid=\"8\">&nbsp;<!-- -->8<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"8\">Tua ahih manin kisikkikna tawh a kilawm gah na gah un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"9\"><sup data-verseid=\"9\">&nbsp;<!-- -->9<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"9\">Note lungsim sungah, ‘Ka pa uh Abraham hi,’ ci in kimuang kha kei un. Banghang hiam cihleh ken kong cih in ah Pasian in hih suangte nangawn Abraham tate a suaksak thei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"10\"><sup data-verseid=\"10\">&nbsp;<!-- -->10<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"10\">Tu mahmah in zong singphung tengah hei kinga zo hi. Tua ahih manin gah hoih a gahlo singkung khempeuh kiphuk in meikuang sungah kikhul ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"11\"><sup data-verseid=\"11\">&nbsp;<!-- -->11<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"11\">“Kisikkikna tungtawn in note tui kong phum hi. Ahi zongin keima khit ciangin a hong pai ding pa in kei sangin vanglian zaw a, ama khedap tawi dingin zong ka kilawm kei hi. Amah in note Kha Siangtho le mei tawh hong phum ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"12\"><sup data-verseid=\"12\">&nbsp;<!-- -->12<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"12\">Amah in a buhcilna tual hahsiang dingin a khutah ansi zapna a tawi hi. Antak teng a ansal sungah sung dinga, ansite ahih leh a mit ngeilo meikuang sungah a khul ding hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"13\"><sup data-verseid=\"13\">&nbsp;<!-- -->13<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"13\">Tua ciangin John tui kiphumsak dingin Galilee gam panin Jordan gunah Zeisu a hong pai hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"14\"><sup data-verseid=\"14\">&nbsp;<!-- -->14<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"14\">Ahih hangin John in, “Nangmah in kei nong tuiphum ding hi zaw napi in banghang in kei kiangah hong pai zawsop na hi hiam?” ci in a mang nuam kei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"15\"><sup data-verseid=\"15\">&nbsp;<!-- -->15<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"15\">Tua ciangin Zeisu in, “Thuman khempeuh i tangtungsak ding kilawm ahih manin tu in hong mang in,” a cih ciangin John in zong a mang hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"16\"><sup data-verseid=\"16\">&nbsp;<!-- -->16<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"16\">Zeisu tui a kiphum khit ciangin tui sung panin a dingto pah hi. Banghang hiam cihleh hellɠ sungah na pumpi bupin hong kikhiat sangin na pumpi nate khat kisia leh a hoih zaw hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"30\"><sup data-verseid=\"30\">&nbsp;<!-- -->30<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"30\">Na taklam khutin hong khialhsak leh sattan inla pai in. Na pumpi bupin hellɠ sungah hong kikhiat sangin na pumpi nate khat kisia leh a hoih zaw hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"31\"><sup data-verseid=\"31\">&nbsp;<!-- -->31<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"31\">“Tua banah, ‘A zi a ma nuam mi peuhmah in, a zi tungah kikhenna lai pia tahen,’ a cihna thu na thei zo uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"32\"><sup data-verseid=\"32\">&nbsp;<!-- -->32<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"32\">Ahih hangin ken kong cih in ah mi khatpeuh in pasal dang tawh a mawhna longal thu dang khatpeuh hangin a zi a mak leh a zi midang tawh a mawh dingin a bawl ahi hi. A kimasa numei a teenpih mi peuhmah zong mi zi tawh a mawh ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"33\"><sup data-verseid=\"33\">&nbsp;<!-- -->33<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"33\">“Tua banah, ‘A manlopi in na kiciam kei dinga, ahi zongin Topa tunga na kamciamte tangtungsak in,’ ci in tanglai mite tunga a kigen thu na thei zo uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"34\"><sup data-verseid=\"34\">&nbsp;<!-- -->34<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"34\">Ahih hangin ken kong cih in ah na kiciam peuhmah kei un. Vantung in Pasian tokhom ahih manin vantung tawh kiciam kei un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"35\"><sup data-verseid=\"35\">&nbsp;<!-- -->35<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"35\">Leitung in ama khengakna ahih manin leitung tawh kiciam kei un. A lian Kumpipa khuapi ahi Jerusalem min tawh kiciam kei un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"36\"><sup data-verseid=\"36\">&nbsp;<!-- -->36<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"36\">Na lutang uh tawh zong kiciam kei in. Banghang hiam cihleh na samzang khat na kangsak, na vomsak thei kei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"37\"><sup data-verseid=\"37\">&nbsp;<!-- -->37<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"37\">Ahi thute, ‘Hi mah hi,’ ci unla, a hilo thute, ‘Hilo hi,’ ci un. Hih zah val in a tam zawk leh gilopa kiang panin a hong piang ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"38\"><sup data-verseid=\"38\">&nbsp;<!-- -->38<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"38\">“ ‘Mittang khat tangin mittang khat, hatang khat tangin hatang khat,’ a cihna thu na zazo uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"39\"><sup data-verseid=\"39\">&nbsp;<!-- -->39<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"39\">Ahih hangin ken kong cih in ah mi gilopa na dokik kei un. Mi khatpeuh in na pang taklam a hong bet leh a langkhat zong na dawh in.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"40\"><sup data-verseid=\"40\">&nbsp;<!-- -->40<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"40\">Mi khatpeuh in na puanak a hong suh nop manin zumah khiat a hong sawm leh na puan tungsilh zong na piak beh in.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"41\"><sup data-verseid=\"41\">&nbsp;<!-- -->41<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"41\">Zawhthawh thu tawh taiɠ khat hong paipih nuamte, tai nih dong na zui in.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"42\"><sup data-verseid=\"42\">&nbsp;<!-- -->42<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"42\">Hong ngente na pia in. Hong leitawi nuamte na nungngat kei in.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"43\"><sup data-verseid=\"43\">&nbsp;<!-- -->43<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"43\">“ ‘Na vengte it inla, na galte mudah in,’ cih thu na zazo uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"44\"><sup data-verseid=\"44\">&nbsp;<!-- -->44<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"44\">Ahi zongin ken kong cih in ah na galte na it un. Hong samsiate thupha na pia un. Hong mudahte tungah thupha na bawl un. A hong simmawh mite le hong bawlsia mite aa dingin thu na ngetsak un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"45\"><sup data-verseid=\"45\">&nbsp;<!-- -->45<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"45\">Tua hi leh vana om na Pa uh tate na hi taktak ding uh hi. Banghang hiam cihleh amah in mihoihlote le mihoihte tungah a kibang in ama ni suaksak a, midikte le midiklote tungah guah zong a zusak tuak hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"46\"><sup data-verseid=\"46\">&nbsp;<!-- -->46<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"46\">Hong itte bek it le uh teh bang lemlawh tuam ding na hi uh hiam? Siahdongte nangawn in zong amau a itte it uh hilo ahi hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"47\"><sup data-verseid=\"47\">&nbsp;<!-- -->47<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"47\">Na lawmte bek maitai le uh teh midangte sangin na hoih zawkna uh bang om tuan ding ahi hiam? Siahdongte nangawn in zong tua bangmah in hih uh hilo ahi hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"48\"><sup data-verseid=\"48\">&nbsp;<!-- -->48<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"48\">Tua ahih ciangin vana om na Pa uh a hoihkim bangin note zong na hoihkim un,” a ci hi.</span></span></div><section class=\"information\"><button class=\"information-toggle\" type=\"button\">Copyrighted Material<!-- -->&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span class=\"learn-more\">Learn More</span><svg class=\"icon\"><use xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" xlink:href=\"/svglist.svg#arrow_down\"></use></svg></button><div aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"rah-static rah-static--height-zero \" style=\"height:0;overflow:hidden\"><div><div style=\"max-height:0\" class=\"copyrights-section\"><div class=\"ot-copyright\"></div><div class=\"nt-copyright\"></div></div></div></div><div class=\"ministry-statement\"><div class=\"ministry-tagline\">©<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"http://www.bible.is\">Bible.is</a>, a ministry of<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.faithcomesbyhearing.com\">Faith Comes By Hearing</a>&nbsp;<!-- -->®.<!-- -->&nbsp;</div><div class=\"ministry-terms-support\"><a id=\"terms-of-service\" href=\"/terms\">Terms and Conditions</a>&nbsp; | &nbsp;<a href=\"https://support.bible.is/contact\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" id=\"help-support\">Help &amp; Support</a></div></div></section></main>",
    "6": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">6</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">“Na hoih na sep uh ciangin mite muh theihtheih dingin na hih khakloh nadingun kidawm un. Tua hi kei leh vantung a om na Pa un thaman a hong pia kei ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">“Tua ahih manin a kitangsam mite huhna na piak uh ciangin a kineihkhem mite piak bangin pia kei un. Aman takpi kong cih in ah, amaute in thaman a ngah zo uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Ahi zongin note in a kitangsam mite huhna na piak uh ciangin na taklam khut tawh na piakte uh na veilam khut theisak kei un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Tua hi leh a kitangsam mite na huhnate uh kilangkhia lo dinga a kilanglote a mu na Pa un a kilangtang in thaman hong pia ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">“Thu na nget uh ciangin zong a kineihkhem mite hih bangin hih kei un. Amaute in mite muh theihtheih dingin kikhopna innte le lamkabom khawng ah dinga, thunget ding a ut uh hi. Aman takpi kong cih in ah, amaute in thaman a ngah zo uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"6\"><sup data-verseid=\"6\">&nbsp;<!-- -->6<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"6\">Note in thu na nget uh ciangin inndei sungah lut unla kong na khak khit uh ciangin a kilanglo a om na Pa uh kiangah ngen un. Tua hi leh a kilanglote a mu na Pa un a kilangtang in thaman hong pia ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"7\"><sup data-verseid=\"7\">&nbsp;<!-- -->7<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"7\">Thu na nget uh ciangin lawkite bangin na gen sasa uh gen phapha kei un. Amaute in gen pha kikkik le uh a ngahdeuh ding kisa uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"8\"><sup data-verseid=\"8\">&nbsp;<!-- -->8<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"8\">Tua ahih manin amaute bang hi kei un. Banghang hiam cihleh na Pa un na kisapnate uh na ngetma un a thei khinzo hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"9\"><sup data-verseid=\"9\">&nbsp;<!-- -->9<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"9\">“Tua ahih manin hih bangin thu na ngen un, Vantung a om kote Pa aw, Na min siangtho kizahtak hen.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"10\"><sup data-verseid=\"10\">&nbsp;<!-- -->10<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"10\">Na kumpigam hong piang tahen. Vantung ah na deihna a kisep mah bangin, Leitung ah zong kisem tahen.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"11\"><sup data-verseid=\"11\">&nbsp;<!-- -->11<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"11\">Tuni a ka nek ding uh an hong pia in.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"12\"><sup data-verseid=\"12\">&nbsp;<!-- -->12<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"12\">Ko tunga hong khialte ka maisak uh bangin, Kote khialhna zong hong maisak ta in.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"13\"><sup data-verseid=\"13\">&nbsp;<!-- -->13<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"13\">Ze‑etna sungah hong lutsak kei inla, Gilopa kiang panin hong honkhia in. Banghang hiam cihleh ukzawhna, Vangliatna le minthanna, Nang aa ahi tawntung hi. Amen.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"14\"><sup data-verseid=\"14\">&nbsp;<!-- -->14<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"14\">“Mite khialhnate na maisak uh leh vana om na Pa un zong note khialhnate hong maisak ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"15\"><sup data-verseid=\"15\">&nbsp;<!-- -->15<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"15\">Mite khialhnate na maisak kei uh leh na Pa un zong note khialhna hong maisak lo ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"16\"><sup data-verseid=\"16\">&nbsp;<!-- -->16<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"16\">“Tua banah an na tan uh ciangin, a kineihkhem mite bangin na mai uh vulsak kei un. Banghang hiam cihleh amaute in antang ahihna uh mite mai ah a kilat theih nadingin a maipuak uh a khel uh hi. Aman takpi kong cih in ah, amaute in thaman a ngah zo uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"17\"><sup data-verseid=\"17\">&nbsp;<!-- -->17<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"17\">Ahi zongin note in an na tan uh ciangin na lu uh sathau nilh unla na mai uh phiat un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"18\"><sup data-verseid=\"18\">&nbsp;<!-- -->18<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"18\">Tua hi leh na antan lam uh mite mai ah kilang lo dinga, a kilanglo a om na Pa uh mai bekah a kilang ding hi. Tua ciangin a kilanglote a mu na Pa un a kilangtang in thaman a hong pia ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"19\"><sup data-verseid=\"19\">&nbsp;<!-- -->19<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"19\">“Na sum na paite uh nget in a nek theihna, a kekseu theihna le gutate in luh in a guk theihna hih leitung ah khol kei un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"20\"><sup data-verseid=\"20\">&nbsp;<!-- -->20<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"20\">Nget in a nek theih lohna, a kekseu theih lohna, gutate in luhin a guk theih lohna vantung ah khol zaw un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"21\"><sup data-verseid=\"21\">&nbsp;<!-- -->21<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"21\">Banghang hiam cihleh na sum a omna munah na lungsim zong a om ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"22\"><sup data-verseid=\"22\">&nbsp;<!-- -->22<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"22\">“Mittang in pumpi aa dingin meivak ahi hi. Tua ahih manin na mit a ciim leh na pumpi bup a vak ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"23\"><sup data-verseid=\"23\">&nbsp;<!-- -->23<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"23\">Ahih hangin na mit a mial leh na pumpi bup a mial ding hi. Tua ahih manin na sunga om khuavak pen khuamial hi leh a nak mial mahmah ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"24\"><sup data-verseid=\"24\">&nbsp;<!-- -->24<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"24\">“Kuamah in to nih na semkhawm zolo hi. Banghang hiam cihleh khat mudah in khat a it ding hi. Ahih keileh khat tungah kipia in khat a simmawh ding hi. Note in Pasian aa ding le sum le pai aa dingin na na semkhawm zo kei ding uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"25\"><sup data-verseid=\"25\">&nbsp;<!-- -->25<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"25\">“Tua ahih manin note kianga kong cih in ah, bang ne in bang dawn ding ka hi hiam ci in nuntak nading lunghimawh kei un. Bang silh bang teeng ding ka hi hiam ci in pumpi aa ding lunghimawh kei un. Nek le dawn sangin nuntakna thupi zaw a, silh le teen sangin pumpi thupi zaw hilo ahi hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"26\"><sup data-verseid=\"26\">&nbsp;<!-- -->26<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"26\">Vana leng vasate en dih un. Amaute in khaici tuh lo, an zong la loin bem le salah zong an a khol kei uh hi. Ahi zongin, vana om na Pa un amaute an a vak hi. Vasate sangin manpha zaw hilo na hi uh hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"27\"><sup data-verseid=\"27\">&nbsp;<!-- -->27<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"27\">Na lunghimawh manun na tun uh tong khat nangawn a behlap thei kua om na hi uh hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"28\"><sup data-verseid=\"28\">&nbsp;<!-- -->28<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"28\">“Tua ahih leh banghang in puansilh ding lunghimawh na hi uh hiam? Gamlak a unokpakte khankhiatzia ngaihsun dih un. Amaute in na sem loin khau zong khek lo uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"29\"><sup data-verseid=\"29\">&nbsp;<!-- -->29<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"29\">Ahih hangin ken kong cih in ah Solomon in a minthanna puan tawh kizem a a om laitak nangawn in hih pakte khat zahin hoih zo nailo hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"30\"><sup data-verseid=\"30\">&nbsp;<!-- -->30<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"30\">Upna neu mite aw, tuni in oma zingciang in meikhuk ah a kikhul ding gamlak a pakte nangawn Pasian in tua bangin puansilh guan ahih leh note hong limguat zawkan ding hilo ahi hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"31\"><sup data-verseid=\"31\">&nbsp;<!-- -->31<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"31\">Tua ahih manin, ‘Bang ka ne dinga, bang ka dawn ding hiam, bang silh dinga bang teeng ding ka hi hiam?’ ci in lunghimawh kei un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"32\"><sup data-verseid=\"32\">&nbsp;<!-- -->32<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"32\">Gentile‑te in hih thute khempeuh a zon pipen uh ahi hi. Vana om na Pa un hih na khempeuh na kisap lam uh a hong thei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"33\"><sup data-verseid=\"33\">&nbsp;<!-- -->33<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"33\">Tua ahih manin Pasian kumpigam le ama dikna zong masa un.     "7": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">7</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">“Thukhenna na thuak loh nadingun midangte tungah thu na khen kei un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Banghang hiam cihleh midangte tunga thu na khen bangun no tungah zong thu hong kikhen ding hi. Note zat tehna tektek mah tawh note aa dingin a hong kitehsakkik ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">“Nangma mita singluang phawk kha loin banghang in na sanggampa mita ninthem muhsak na hi hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Ngaihsun dih in na mit ah singluang khat om napi banghang in na sanggampa kiangah, ‘Na mita ninthem hong lakkhiatsak ning,’ ci thei na hi hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">A kineihkhem mipa aw! Nangma mita singluang lakhia masa in. Tua hi leh na sanggampa mita ninthem telmuh in na lakkhiatsak thei pan ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"6\"><sup data-verseid=\"6\">&nbsp;<!-- -->6<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"6\">“A siangtho nate uite pia kei un. Kepsuangmanphate zong vokpi mai ah lot kha kei un. Na lotkhak leh a khe tawh tuangawp in kihei in nang a hong petgawp ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"7\"><sup data-verseid=\"7\">&nbsp;<!-- -->7<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"7\">“Ngen un, hong kipia ding hi. Zong un, na mu ding uh hi. Kiu un, hong kihon ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"8\"><sup data-verseid=\"8\">&nbsp;<!-- -->8<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"8\">Banghang hiam cihleh a ngente in ngah a, a zongte in mu in, a kiute kong kihon hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"9\"><sup data-verseid=\"9\">&nbsp;<!-- -->9<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"9\">“Note lakah a ta in anlum ngen leh suang a pia ding,</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"10\"><sup data-verseid=\"10\">&nbsp;<!-- -->10<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"10\">ngasa ngen leh gul a pia ding kua om na hi uh hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"11\"><sup data-verseid=\"11\">&nbsp;<!-- -->11<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"11\">No mihoihlote nangawn in na tate uh na hoih piak ding thei na hih uh leh vana om na Pa un ama kianga a ngente na hoih hong pia zawthamlo ding ahi hiam!</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"12\"><sup data-verseid=\"12\">&nbsp;<!-- -->12<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"12\">Tua ahih manin note tunga hong kibawl dinga na deih khempeuh uh midangte tungah zong na bawl un. Thukham le Kamsangte laibu‑te zong hih thu mah ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"13\"><sup data-verseid=\"13\">&nbsp;<!-- -->13<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"13\">“Kong kawcik ah lut un. Banghang hiam cihleh siatna mun tun nading kongpi zai a, lampi zong tanzau ahih manin mi tampi in tua lampi a tawn uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"14\"><sup data-verseid=\"14\">&nbsp;<!-- -->14<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"14\">Nuntakna mun tun nading kong kawcik a, lampi zong neu ahih manin mi tawmcik bekin a zui uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"15\"><sup data-verseid=\"15\">&nbsp;<!-- -->15<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"15\">“A lungsim tawng uh ngia bangin gilo napi tuuvun silh a, note kianga a hong pai kamsangzuaute na kidawm un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"16\"><sup data-verseid=\"16\">&nbsp;<!-- -->16<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"16\">Amaute bangci mi hiam cih a gah panun na thei ding uh hi. Lingkung panin lenggah kilo thei ahi hiam? Thangling kung panin theigah kilo thei ahi hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"17\"><sup data-verseid=\"17\">&nbsp;<!-- -->17<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"17\">Tua ahih manin singkung hoih leh a gah hoih in singkung hoih kei leh a gah zong a hoih kei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"18\"><sup data-verseid=\"18\">&nbsp;<!-- -->18<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"18\">Singkung hoih in gah hoihlo gah theilo a, singkung hoihlo in gah hoih a gah thei kei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"19\"><sup data-verseid=\"19\">&nbsp;<!-- -->19<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"19\">Gah hoih a gahlo singkung khempeuh kiphuk in meikuang sungah kikhul ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"20\"><sup data-verseid=\"20\">&nbsp;<!-- -->20<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"20\">Tua ahih manin amaute bangci mi hiam cih a gah panun na thei ding uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"21\"><sup data-verseid=\"21\">&nbsp;<!-- -->21<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"21\">“ ‘Topa aw, Topa aw,’ hong ci peuhmah vantung kumpigam sungah a lutkim kei ding uh hi. Vana ka Pa deih banga a gamtate bek a lut ding uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"22\"><sup data-verseid=\"22\">&nbsp;<!-- -->22<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"22\">Tua ni ciangin mi tampi in, ‘Topa aw, Topa aw, nangma min tawh kamsang in thugen hilo ka hi uh hiam? Nangma min tawh dawite hawlkhia in nangma min tawh nalamdang bawl hilo ka hi uh hiam?’ hong ci ding uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"23\"><sup data-verseid=\"23\">&nbsp;<!-- -->23<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"23\">Tua ciangin, ‘Note kong thei ngei kei hi. Siatna a bawl mite aw, ka kiang panin paikhia un!’ ka ci ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"24\"><sup data-verseid=\"24\">&nbsp;<!-- -->24<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"24\">“Tua ahih manin hih ka thugente za‑a a zui mi khatpeuh in suangpi tunga innlam mipilpa tawh kibang hi ci in ka gen ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"25\"><sup data-verseid=\"25\">&nbsp;<!-- -->25<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"25\">Guahzu in tui hong khang a, huihpi nungin tua inn a nawk hangin suangpi tungah kilam ahih manin a puk kei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"26\"><sup data-verseid=\"26\">&nbsp;<!-- -->26<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"26\">Hih ka thugente za napi in a zuilo mi in, sehnel tunga innlam mihaipa tawh kibang hi ci in ka gen ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"27\"><sup data-verseid=\"27\">&nbsp;<!-- -->27<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"27\">Guahzu in tui hong khang a, huihpi nungin tua inn a nawk ciangin a puk hi. Tua pukna in a lian mahmah pukna ahi hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"28\"><sup data-verseid=\"28\">&nbsp;<!-- -->28<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"28\">Zeisu in hih thute a gen khit ciangin mihonpite in a thuhilhna lamdang a sa mahmah uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"29\"><sup data-verseid=\"29\">&nbsp;<!-- -->29<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"29\">Banghang hiam cihleh thukhamhilh siate bangin hilh loin thuneipa bangin a hilh hi.</span></span></div><section class=\"information\"><button class=\"information-toggle\" type=\"button\">Copyrighted Material<!-- -->&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span class=\"learn-more\">Learn More</span><svg class=\"icon\"><use xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" xlink:href=\"/svglist.svg#arrow_down\"></use></svg></button><div aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"rah-static rah-static--height-zero \" style=\"height:0;overflow:hidden\"><div><div style=\"max-height:0\" class=\"copyrights-section\"><div class=\"ot-copyright\"></div><div class=\"nt-copyright\"></div></div></div></div><div class=\"ministry-statement\"><div class=\"ministry-tagline\">©<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"http://www.bible.is\">Bible.is</a>, a ministry of<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.faithcomesbyhearing.com\">Faith Comes By Hearing</a>&nbsp;<!-- -->®.<!-- -->&nbsp;</div><div class=\"ministry-terms-support\"><a id=\"terms-of-service\" href=\"/terms\">Terms and Conditions</a>&nbsp; | &nbsp;<a href=\"https://support.bible.is/contact\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" id=\"help-support\">Help &amp; Support</a></div></div></section></main>",
    "8": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">8</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Zeisu mualtung pan hong kumsuk khit ciangin mihonpite in amah a zui uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Tua ciangin, en in, miphak khat hong pai in amah bia a, “Topa aw, hong damsak nuam lecin nong damsak thei hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Zeisu in a khut zanin amah lawng a, “Kong damsak nuam hi, damta in,” ci a, thu a piak ciangin thakhat in a dam pah hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Tua ciangin Zeisu in ama kiangah, “Hih thu kuama kiangah gen kei in. Ka nasempa kiangah, ‘Hih sem in,’ ka cih ciangin a sem hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"10\"><sup data-verseid=\"10\">&nbsp;<!-- -->10<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"10\">Zeisu in tua thu a zak ciangin lamdangsa mahmah a, amah a zui mite kiangah, “Aman takpi kong cih in ah, Israel mite lak nangawn ah hi zahtak a lian upna a nei ka mu ngei kei hi!</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"11\"><sup data-verseid=\"11\">&nbsp;<!-- -->11<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"11\">Ken kong cih in ah nisuahna le nitumna lam panin mi tampi hong pai in Abraham, Isaac le Jacob‑te tawh vantung kumpigam sungah a tukhawm ding uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"12\"><sup data-verseid=\"12\">&nbsp;<!-- -->12<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"12\">Ahi zongin tua kumpigam tate ahih leh a pualam khuamial lakah a lawnkhia ding hi. Zeisu in amaute upna a muh ciangin pumzawpa kiangah, “Ka ta aw, lungnuam in na mawhnate hong kimaisak zo hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Tua thu a zak phetun thukhamhilh siate pawlkhat in a lungsim uh ah, “Hihpa Pasian tungah a pausia hi!” a ci pah uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Zeisu in amaute lungsim thei ahih manin, “Banghang in note lungsim sungah thusia ngaihsun na hi uh hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">‘Na mawhnate hong kimaisak zo hi,’ cih ding le, ‘Tho inla lampai in,’ cih ding koi baih zaw ahi hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"6\"><sup data-verseid=\"6\">&nbsp;<!-- -->6<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"6\">Ahi zongin Mihing Tapa in leitung ah mawhmaisak theihna thu a neih lam na theih nadingun,” a cih khit ciangin pumzawpa kiangah, “Tho in, na lupna pua inla, na inn ah ciah in,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"8\"><sup data-verseid=\"8\">&nbsp;<!-- -->8<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"8\">Mihonpite in hih thupiang a muh uh ciangin, lamdangsa mahmah uh a, mihingte tungah tua bang vangliatna a pia Pasian a phat uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"9\"><sup data-verseid=\"9\">&nbsp;<!-- -->9<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"9\">Tua mun panin Zeisu paisuak a, siahdonna buuk sunga a tu Matthew kici mi khat a muh ciangin, “Hong zui in,” a ci hi. Matthew zong dingkhia in Zeisu a zui hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"10\"><sup data-verseid=\"10\">&nbsp;<!-- -->10<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"10\">Inn sungah Zeisu an ne‑a a tut laitak in, en in, siahdongte le mawhneite tampitak hong pai in Zeisu le a nungzuite tawh ankuang a umkhawm uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"11\"><sup data-verseid=\"11\">&nbsp;<!-- -->11<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"11\">Pharisee pawlte in a muh uh ciangin a nungzuite kiangah, “Banghang in na siapa un siahdongte le mawhneite tawh an nekhawm ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"12\"><sup data-verseid=\"12\">&nbsp;<!-- -->12<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"12\">Tua thu a zak ciangin Zeisu in amaute kiangah, “Mi cidamte aa dingin siavuan kisam lo a, mi cinate aa ding bekin kisam hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"13\"><sup data-verseid=\"13\">&nbsp;<!-- -->13<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"13\">Ahih hangin va pai unla, ‘Gangawh biakna sangin hehpihna ka deih zaw hi,’ a cihna thu a khiatna va kantel phot un. Banghang hiam cihleh midikte sam dinga hong pai ka hi kei hi. Mawhneite a kisikkik theih nadingun a sam dinga hong pai ka hi hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"14\"><sup data-verseid=\"14\">&nbsp;<!-- -->14<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"14\">Tua khit ciangin John nungzuite a kiangah hong pai uh a, “Kote le Pharisee pawlte in an ka tang zelzel uh hi. Banghang in na nungzuite in antang lo uh ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"15\"><sup data-verseid=\"15\">&nbsp;<!-- -->15<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"15\">Tua ciangin Zeisu in, “Zineipa tawh a omkhop sungun a lawm a gualte thum le tau in ombuang ding uh ahi hiam? Ahih hangin amaute kiang pan zineipa a kilakkhiat hun hong tung dinga, tua ciangin bel an a tang ding uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"16\"><sup data-verseid=\"16\">&nbsp;<!-- -->16<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"16\">“Puan lui a kiphop ciangin kuamah in a ton nailo puanbek a thak tawh a phop kei hi. Tua bangin phop leh a phopna puanbek a thak in puan lui kaikek in, a kekna a zai semsem ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"17\"><sup data-verseid=\"17\">&nbsp;<!-- -->17<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"17\">Kuamah in savun um lui sungah lenggahtui thak a thun kei hi. Tua hi leh a nih tuakin bitkhawm in sawtveipi kikoih thei hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"18\"><sup data-verseid=\"18\">&nbsp;<!-- -->18<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"18\">Hih thute a gengen laitak in, en in, makaipa khat hong pai in amah bia a, “Ka tanu tu mahmah in a si hi. Ahi zongin nang hong pai in a tungah na khut nga leteh a hing ding hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"19\"><sup data-verseid=\"19\">&nbsp;<!-- -->19<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"19\">Zeisu dingkhia in amah zui a, a nungzuite in zong a zui uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"20\"><sup data-verseid=\"20\">&nbsp;<!-- -->20<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"20\">Tua laitak in kum sawm le kum nih sung tawntung siluang natna a vei numei khatin Zeisu nunglam panin a puanmongtep thakhat in a va lawng hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"21\"><sup data-verseid=\"21\">&nbsp;<!-- -->21<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"21\">Amah in a lungsim sungah, “A puan va lawng beek leng zong ka dam ding hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"22\"><sup data-verseid=\"22\">&nbsp;<!-- -->22<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"22\">Zeisu a nunglam ah kihei a, amah a muh ciangin, “Ka tanu aw, lungnuam in, na upna in a hong damsak zo hi,” a ci hi. Tua hun lian mahin tua numei a dam hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"23\"><sup data-verseid=\"23\">&nbsp;<!-- -->23<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"23\">Makaipa inn sungah Zeisu a lut ciangin tamngai tumte le kap a gamlum ngeingai mihonpi a mu hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"24\"><sup data-verseid=\"24\">&nbsp;<!-- -->24<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"24\">Tua ciangin amah in tua mite kiangah, “Na awn un. Numeino a si hilo in a ihmu ahi hi,” a cih leh amaute in zahpih in a nuihsan uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"25\"><sup data-verseid=\"25\">&nbsp;<!-- -->25<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"25\">Ahih hangin Zeisu in mihonpi a pusuahsak khit ciangin inn sungah lut a, numeino khut a let ciangin numeino a tho hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"26\"><sup data-verseid=\"26\">&nbsp;<!-- -->26<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"26\">Hih thu tua gam mun khempeuh ah a kizel hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"27\"><sup data-verseid=\"27\">&nbsp;<!-- -->27<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"27\">Tua mun pan Zeisu a paikhiat ciangin, mittaw nih in amah zui uh a, “David Tapa aw, kote hong hehpih in!” ci in a kiko uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"28\"><sup data-verseid=\"28\">&nbsp;<!-- -->28<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"28\">Inn sungah amah a lut ciangin, mittaw nihte in zong a zui uh hi. Zeisu in amaute kiangah, “Hih thu kuamah theisak peuhmah kei un,” ci in khauhtak in thu a pia hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"31\"><sup data-verseid=\"31\">&nbsp;<!-- -->31<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"31\">Ahih hangin amaute paikhia uh a, tua gam sung khempeuh ah ama thu a kizelsak uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"32\"><sup data-verseid=\"32\">&nbsp;<!-- -->32<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"32\">Tua mi nihte a paikhiat laitak mah un, en in, a pautheilo dawilut mi khat ama kiangah hong paipih uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"33\"><sup data-verseid=\"33\">&nbsp;<!-- -->33<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"33\">Amah in dawi a hawlkhiat ciangin, a pautheilo pa hong pauthei pah hi. Mihonpi in lamdangsa mahmah uh a, “Israel mite lakah hih bang i mu ngei kei hi!” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"34\"><sup data-verseid=\"34\">&nbsp;<!-- -->34<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"34\">Ahih hangin, Pharisee‑te in, “Amah in dawi mangpipa min suangin dawigilote a hawlkhia ahi hi,” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"35\"><sup data-verseid=\"35\">&nbsp;<!-- -->35<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"35\">Tua bangin khuapi khuata kici tengah Zeisu vak kawikawi in amaute kikhopna innte ah thu a hilh hi. Pasian kumpigam lungdamna thu tangko in cina le natna tuamtuam a nei mi khempeuh a damsak hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"36\"><sup data-verseid=\"36\">&nbsp;<!-- -->36<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"36\">Amah in mihonpite a et ciangin hehpihhuai a sa mahmah hi. style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"36\"><sup data-verseid=\"36\">&nbsp;<!-- -->36<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"36\">Mi khat galin ama Tua ahih ciangin amaute in note tungah thu a hong khente a suak ding uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"28\"><sup data-verseid=\"28\">&nbsp;<!-- -->28<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"28\">Ahih hangin Pasian Kha tawh dawite hawlkhia ka hih manin note tungah Pasian kumpigam hong tung zo hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"29\"><sup data-verseid=\"29\">&nbsp;<!-- -->29<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"29\">Ahih keileh mi khatin mi thahat khat hencip masa lopi in a inn luhin a neih a lamte bangci laksak thei ding ahi hiam? Tang ahih leh ka ansal ah hong sung un,” ci in ka vaikhak ding hi,’ ” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"31\"><sup data-verseid=\"31\">&nbsp;<!-- -->31<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"31\">Amah in gentehna dang khat a gen in ah, “Vantung kumpigam in mi khatin lolai a a vawh ankamtang tawh kibang hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"32\"><sup data-verseid=\"32\">&nbsp;<!-- -->32<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"32\">Ankamtang in khaici tang khempeuh lakah a neupen ahih hangin a khan khit ciangin anteh kung dangte sangin golzaw a, a kung lianpi khat hong suak hi.     "17": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">17</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Ni guk khit ciangin Zeisu in Peter, James le a sanggampa John‑te samin mualsang khat tungah amau teng bek a paipih hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Amaute mai ah ama mel kikhel in a maitang ni bangin tanga a puante khuavak bangin a tee hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">En in, amaute kiangah Moses le Elijah hong kilang in Zeisu tawh a kiho uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Tua ciangin Peter in Zeisu kiangah, “Topa aw, hihlai nuam ka sa uh hi. Ka kibaptize na ah kibaptize zo ding na hi uh hiam?” a cih ciangin amaute in, “Hi zo mah nung,” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"23\"><sup data-verseid=\"23\">&nbsp;<!-- -->23<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"23\">Tua ciangin amah in, “Ka dawn ding hai na dawn takpi ding uh a, ka kibaptize na ah zong na kibaptize takpi ding uh hi. Ahih hangin ka taklam le ka veilam a tut theih nading thu pen kei hong piak theih hilo in ka Pa in a sehkholhsa mite aa ding ahi hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"24\"><sup data-verseid=\"24\">&nbsp;<!-- -->24<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"24\">A dang sawmte in tua thu a zak uh ciangin tua unau nihte tungah a lungkim kei uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"25\"><sup data-verseid=\"25\">&nbsp;<!-- -->25<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"25\">Ahi zongin Zeisu in amaute samkhawm a, “Gentile‑te sungah ukna neite in a mipite uh ukcip uh a, a miliante un a mipite tungah thuneihna zang uh hi cih na thei uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"26\"><sup data-verseid=\"26\">&nbsp;<!-- -->26<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"26\">Ahi zongin note sungah tua bang ding hilo hi. Note lakah a lian a suak nuam mite in note nasem hi tahen.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"27\"><sup data-verseid=\"27\">&nbsp;<!-- -->27<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"27\">Note lakah a masa pen a suak nuamte in note sila hi tahen.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"28\"><sup data-verseid=\"28\">&nbsp;<!-- -->28<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"28\">Mihing Tapa nangawn ama na a kisepsak dinga hong pai hilo hi. Midangte na a sepsak ding le a nuntakna pia in mi tampi a tankhia dinga hong pai ahi hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"29\"><sup data-verseid=\"29\">&nbsp;<!-- -->29<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"29\">Jericho khua pan a paikhiat uh ciangin mihonpi in Zeisu nung a zui uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"30\"><sup data-verseid=\"30\">&nbsp;<!-- -->30<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"30\">Tua ciangin lamgei a tu mittaw nihin amaute lamah Zeisu hong pai hi cih a zak uh ciangin, “David Tapa, Topa aw, kote hong hehpih in,” ci in a kiko uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"31\"><sup data-verseid=\"31\">&nbsp;<!-- -->31<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"31\">Amaute a daih nadingun mihonpi in a taiihuan uh hi. Ahih hangin amaute in, “David Tapa, Topa aw, kote hong hehpih in,” ci in nakpi in a kiko semsem uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"32\"><sup data-verseid=\"32\">&nbsp;<!-- -->32<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"32\">Tua ciangin Zeisu a dinsa in khawla amaute sam in, “Bang kong hihsak ding ut na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"33\"><sup data-verseid=\"33\">&nbsp;<!-- -->33<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"33\">Amaute in, “Topa aw, khua nong muhsak ding ka ut uh hi,” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"34\"><sup data-verseid=\"34\">&nbsp;<!-- -->34<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"34\">Zeisu in amaute hehpihhuai sa in a mit uh a lawnsak leh thakhat in khua mu pah uh a, ama nung a zui uh hi.</span></span></div><section class=\"information\"><button class=\"information-toggle\" type=\"button\">Copyrighted Material<!-- -->&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span class=\"learn-more\">Learn     "21": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">21</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Jerusalem khuapi tun kuan, Tanluan mual kianga om Bethphage khua a tun uh ciangin Zeisu in a nungzuite nih sawl a,</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">“Note mai‑a khua ah va lut un. Laapi khat kikhih a om na mu pah ding uha a no zong a kiangah na om ding hi. Suut unla hong kai un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Mi khatpeuh in hong paupih leh, ‘Topa in amaute zang nuam hi, hong puakkik pah ding hi,’ ci un,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Hih thute khempeuh in kamsangpa gensa thute a tangtun nadinga piang ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">Amah in, “ ‘En in, laapi ta laano tungah tuangin, Na Kumpipa lungnemtak in, Nang kiangah hong pai hi,’ ci in, Zion tanu kiangah gen in,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"6\"><sup data-verseid=\"6\">&nbsp;<!-- -->6<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"6\">Tua ciangin nungzuite gel zong pai uh a, Zeisu thupiak bangin ahih uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"7\"><sup data-verseid=\"7\">&nbsp;<!-- -->7<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"7\">Laapi le laano hong kai uha tuate tungah a puante uh phahin Zeisu a tuangsak uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"8\"><sup data-verseid=\"8\">&nbsp;<!-- -->8<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"8\">Mihon tampitak in a puante uh lampi ah phah uh hi. Pawlkhatte in singhiangte satin phah uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"9\"><sup data-verseid=\"9\">&nbsp;<!-- -->9<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"9\">A nung le a mai‑a a pai mihonpite kiko uh a, “David Tapa tungah Hosannaɠ! Topa min tawh a hong paipa in, Thupha ngah tahen! A sangbel munah Hosanna!” ci in a kiko uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"10\"><sup data-verseid=\"10\">&nbsp;<!-- -->10<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"10\">Jerusalem khuapi sung a lut ciangin khuapi sunga om mi khempeuh ciak ngeingai uh a, “Hihpa kua ahi hiam?” ci in khat le khat a kidong uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"11\"><sup data-verseid=\"11\">&nbsp;<!-- -->11<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"11\">Mihonpi in, “Galilee gam Nazareth khua mi kamsangpa Zeisu ahi hi,” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"12\"><sup data-verseid=\"12\">&nbsp;<!-- -->12<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"12\">Tua khit ciangin Pasian biakinnpi huang sungah Zeisu lut a, biakinnpi huang sungah vanlei, vanzuak a om mi khempeuh a hawlkhia hi. Sumkhekteɠ sabuaite le vakhu zuakte tutphahte zong a lumletsak hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"13\"><sup data-verseid=\"13\">&nbsp;<!-- -->13<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"13\">Tua khit ciangin amaute kiangah, “ ‘Ka inn in thungetna inn kici ding hi,’ ahih hangin note in ‘gutate phualpi’ na suaksak uh hi ci in Lai Siangtho sungah kigelh hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"14\"><sup data-verseid=\"14\">&nbsp;<!-- -->14<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"14\">Biakinnpi huang sunga a om laitak in ama kiangah mittawte le khebaite hong pai uh a, amah in amaute a damsak hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"15\"><sup data-verseid=\"15\">&nbsp;<!-- -->15<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"15\">Siampi liante le thukhamhilh siate in ama bawl nalamdangte mu in, “David Tapa tungah Hosannaɠ!” ci in biakinnpi huang sunga a om naupangnote kikona aw a zak uh ciangin a heh mahmah uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"16\"><sup data-verseid=\"16\">&nbsp;<!-- -->16<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"16\">Tua ciangin ama kiangah, “Hih naupangte kikona aw na za hiam?” a ci uh hi. Zeisu in amaute kiangah, “Ka za hi, ‘Naupangnote le nawine naungekte kam panin phatna kicing na gingkhiasak hi,’ a cihna thu sim ngeilo na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"17\"><sup data-verseid=\"17\">&nbsp;<!-- -->17<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"17\">Tua khit ciangin amaute nusia in khuapi sung pan Bethany khualam zuanin paikhia a, tua khua ah a giak hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"18\"><sup data-verseid=\"18\">&nbsp;<!-- -->18<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"18\">Zingsang tungin khuapi lam zuanin Zeisu hong paikik a, lamkal ah a gilkial hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"19\"><sup data-verseid=\"19\">&nbsp;<!-- -->19<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"19\">Lamgei ah theikung khat mu in a phungah a va pai leh a teh longal bangmah a mu kei hi. Tua ciangin Zeisu in, “Tu a kipan gah ngei nawn peuhmah kei in,” a cih ciangin tua theikung thakhat in a keugaw hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"20\"><sup data-verseid=\"20\">&nbsp;<!-- -->20<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"20\">Nungzuite in a muh uh ciangin, lamdangsa mahmah uh a, “Banghang in hih theikung keugaw pah zawzen ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"21\"><sup data-verseid=\"21\">&nbsp;<!-- -->21<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"21\">Zeisu in amaute kiangah, “Aman takpi kong cih in ah, lunghiang loin um taktak le uh teh hih theikung tunga thupiang bang bek hilo in hih mualpi kiangah zong, ‘Kihemkhia inla tuipi sung kidenna in,’ ci le uh cin tua bangin a piang ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"22\"><sup data-verseid=\"22\">&nbsp;<!-- -->22<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"22\">Upna tawh na nget uh leh na nget peuhpeuh uh a vekpi in na ngah ding uh hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"23\"><sup data-verseid=\"23\">&nbsp;<!-- -->23<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"23\">Biakinnpi huang sungah Zeisu lutin thu a hilh laitak in siampi liante le Judah mite makaite ama kiangah va pai uh a, “Hih bang nate na sep theih nadingin kua kiang panin thu ngah na hi hiam? Hih thuneihna kua in nang hong pia ahi hiam?” ci in a dong uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"24\"><sup data-verseid=\"24\">&nbsp;<!-- -->24<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"24\">Zeisu in, “Ken zong note thukhat kong dong ding hi. Nong dawn theih uh leh hih nate kua thuneihna tawh hih ka hi hiam cih kong gen pan ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"25\"><sup data-verseid=\"25\">&nbsp;<!-- -->25<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"25\">John tuiphumna thu vantung pana thuneihna tawh ahi hiam, mihing pana thuneihna tawh ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin amaute kikum uh a, “ ‘Vantung pana thuneihna tawh hi,’ ci lehang, ‘Tua ahih leh banghang in amah um lo na hi uh hiam?’ hong ci ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"26\"><sup data-verseid=\"26\">&nbsp;<!-- -->26<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"26\">‘Mihing thuneihna tawh hi,’ ci lehang lah mi khempeuh in John pen kamsangpa a a san khitsa uh ahih manin mihonte kihtakhuai hi,” a kici uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"27\"><sup data-verseid=\"27\">&nbsp;<!-- -->27<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"27\">Tua ahih manin, “Ka thei kei uh hi,” ci in a dawng uh hi. Tua ciangin Zeisu in, “Ken zong hih nate kua thuneihna tawh sem ka hi hiam cih kong gen kei ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"28\"><sup data-verseid=\"28\">&nbsp;<!-- -->28<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"28\">“Ahi zongin hih kong gen ding thu bang na ci ngaihsut uh hiam? Mi khatin tapa nih a nei hi. A ta uzawpa kiangah va pai a, ‘Ka ta aw, tuni in ka lenggah lo ah va kuan in,’ a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"29\"><sup data-verseid=\"29\">&nbsp;<!-- -->29<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"29\">“Tua a tapa in, ‘Ka kuan nuam kei hi,’ a cih hangin a nung ciangin kisikkik in a kuan hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"30\"><sup data-verseid=\"30\">&nbsp;<!-- -->30<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"30\">“Tua khit ciangin a nauzawpa kiangah pai a, tuamah bangin a gen hi. A tapa in, ‘Pa aw, ka kuan ding hi,’ ci in dawng napi a kuan kei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"31\"><sup data-verseid=\"31\">&nbsp;<!-- -->31<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"31\">“Tua ta nihte kua zaw in a pa deihna mang ahi hiam?” a cih ciangin amaute in, “A upapen in a mang zaw hi,” a ci uh hi. Zeisu in amaute kiangah, “Aman takpi kong cih in ah, siahdongte le numei kizuakte in Pasian kumpigam sungah note ma in a lut uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"32\"><sup data-verseid=\"32\">&nbsp;<!-- -->32<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"32\">Banghang hiam cihleh John hong pai in thuman lampi hong lah hangin amah na um kei uh hi. Ahi zongin siahdongte le numei kizuakte in amah a um uh hi. Note in hih thu na muh khit nangawn un kisik in amah na um tuan kei uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"33\"><sup data-verseid=\"33\">&nbsp;<!-- -->33<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"33\">“A dang thugentehna khat na ngai un. Leitang neipa khatin lenggah lo khat bawl in a kim ah phung ciangin um a, lenggah cilna phual khat bawl in buuktau khat zong a dawh hi. Tua khit ciangin lenggah lo kho dingin mi cial a, khual gamlapi khatah a zinkhia hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"34\"><sup data-verseid=\"34\">&nbsp;<!-- -->34<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"34\">Tu in lenggah lak hun hong naita a, lenggahte a kaikhawm dingin lokhawh thalawhte kiangah a nasemte a sawl hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"35\"><sup data-verseid=\"35\">&nbsp;<!-- -->35<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"35\">“Lokhawh thalawhte in a nasemte man uh a, khat vuagawp in khat that uh a, a dang khat pen suang tawh a denglum uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"36\"><sup data-verseid=\"36\">&nbsp;<!-- -->36<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"36\">Tua ciangin loneipa in a sawl masakte sangin a tam zaw a nasemte pawlkhat sawlkik leuleu a, tuate zong a masate a bawl mah bangun a bawl veve uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"37\"><sup data-verseid=\"37\">&nbsp;<!-- -->37<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"37\">A tawpna ah loneipa in, ‘Ka tapa zahtak kha ding uh hi,’ ci in a tapa a paisak hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"38\"><sup data-verseid=\"38\">&nbsp;<!-- -->38<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"38\">“Ahih hangin lokhawh thalawhte in a tapa a muh uh ciangin kikum uh a, ‘Hihpa innluah ding pa ahi hi. Pai dih un, amah thatin a luah ding teng sut ni,’ a kici uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"39\"><sup data-verseid=\"39\">&nbsp;<!-- -->39<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"39\">Tua ciangin amah man uh a, lenggah lo pua lamah kaikhia in a that uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"40\"><sup data-verseid=\"40\">&nbsp;<!-- -->40<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"40\">“Tua hi a, lenggah loneipa a hong pai ciangin tua lokhawh thalawhte bang a ci bawl ding hiam?” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"41\"><sup data-verseid=\"41\">&nbsp;<!-- -->41<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"41\">Amaute in, “Amah in tua migilote nasiatak in a susia ding hi. Lenggah lak hun ciangin loneipa tungah lenggah a ngah zah ding a pia ding a dang lokhawh thalawhte a khosak ding hi,” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"42\"><sup data-verseid=\"42\">&nbsp;<!-- -->42<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"42\">Zeisu in amaute kiangah, “ ‘Innlamte in a nilkhiat suang, Innkiusuang bulpi a suak hi. Hih in Topa sep hi a, Eite muhna ah lamdang hi,’ ci in Lai Siangtho sunga a kigelh thu sim ngeilo na hi uh hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"43\"><sup data-verseid=\"43\">&nbsp;<!-- -->43<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"43\">“Tua ahih manin note kianga kong gen in ah, note tung panin Pasian kumpigam kilakhia dinga, a gahsak ding minamdangte khat tungah kipia ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"44\"><sup data-verseid=\"44\">&nbsp;<!-- -->44<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"44\">Hih suang tungah mi khatpeuh a kiat leh kitamkham dinga, hih suangin mi khatpeuh a den leh a zanciim ding hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"45\"><sup data-verseid=\"45\">&nbsp;<!-- -->45<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"45\">Tu in siampi liante le Pharisee pawlte in ama thugentehnate a zak uh ciangin amaute a cihna ahihlam a thei uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"46\"><sup data-verseid=\"46\">&nbsp;<!-- -->46<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"46\">Zeisu mat a sawm uh hangin mihonpi in kamsangpa hi ci in um khin uh ahih manin mihonpi a kihta zel uh hi.</span></span></div><section class=\"information\"><button class=\"information-toggle\"     "28": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">28</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Tu in Sabbath ni a bei khit nipi kal sunga ni masa pen ni zingsang phalvak tungin Magdala khua mi Mary le Mary dang khat daihawh dingin a pai uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Tua ciangin, en in, zin nakpi in hong ling hi.
